| Invited parent: guardianPlayerLink with `acknowledgedByParentAt` | **PASS** | `members.ts:2836, 2868` |
| Self-reg: guardian_claim skipped | **PASS** | `onboarding.ts:241-249` (gated by `wasInvited`) |
| Self-reg: no_children_found removed | **PASS** | Absent from onboarding task creation (US-P0.8-004) |
| Self-reg: redirect to `/orgs/join` | **PASS** | `page.tsx:148-149` |
| `approveJoinRequest` creates guardianIdentity | **PASS** | `orgJoinRequests.ts:434-471` |
| `approveJoinRequest` creates guardianPlayerLinks | **PASS** | `orgJoinRequests.ts:503-520` |

### What's missing:

1. **No automated test file for US-P0.8-008** - File does not exist in `packages/backend/convex/__tests__/`. Other story tests (001, 002, 003, 006) exist but are placeholder stubs only (`expect(true).toBe(true)`).

2. **"All tests pass" criterion unverifiable** - No automated tests to run. A UAT document exists at `scripts/ralph/agents/output/tests/phase-0.8-onboarding-flow-differentiation-US-P0.8-008-uat.md` but there's no evidence it was executed.

3. **"Document any issues found" criterion** - No issues document produced from testing.

### Minor issues noted:

- Dead code: `no-children-found-step.tsx` (338 lines) still exists but is never rendered
- Residual `console.log` statements remain in members.ts, orgJoinRequests.ts, and page.tsx despite US-P0.8-007 cleanup

### Verdict

**PARTIAL** - The underlying implementation for all three test flows is complete and correct. However, the story's own acceptance criteria require tests to actually pass and issues to be documented, and no automated tests exist (only placeholder stubs). Manual UAT has not been evidenced as executed.
